<P class="p27 ft13"><SPAN class="ft5">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft12">Denna lag tr√§der i kraft den dag regeringen best√§mmer och till√§mpas betr√§ffande skatter p√• inkomst, p√• inkomst som f√∂rv√§rvas den 1 januari det √•r som f√∂ljer n√§rmast efter det √•r d√• lagen tr√§der i kraft eller senare.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p30 ft4">Avtal mellan Konungariket Sveriges regering och Republiken Polens regering f√∂r undvikande av dubbelbeskattning och f√∂rhindrande av skatteflykt betr√§ffande skatter p√• inkomst</P>
<P class="p31 ft9">Konungariket Sveriges regering och Republiken Polens regering, som √∂nskar ing√• ett avtal f√∂r undvikande av dubbelbeskattning och f√∂rhindrande av skatteflykt betr√§ffande skatter p√• inkomst, har kommit √∂verens om f√∂ljande:</P>

<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p32 ft4">Bilaga Prop. 2004/05:121</P>
<P class="p33 ft4">Convention between the Government of the Kingdom of Sweden and the Government of the Republic of Poland for the avoidance of double taxation and the prevention of fiscal evasion with respect to taxes on income</P>
<P class="p34 ft4">The Government of the Kingdom of Sweden and the Government of the Republic of Poland, desiring to conclude a Convention for the avoidance of double taxation and the prevention of fiscal evasion with respect to taxes on income, have agreed as follows:</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p35 ft4">Artikel 1</P>
<P class="p36 ft4">Personer p√• vilka avtalet till√§mpas</P>
<P class="p37 ft4">Detta avtal till√§mpas p√• personer som har hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat eller i b√•da avtalsslutande staterna.</P>
<P class="p38 ft4">Artikel 2</P>
<P class="p39 ft4">Skatter som omfattas av avtalet</P>
<P class="p37 ft4">1. De skatter p√• vilka detta avtal till√§mpas √§r:</P>
<P class="p40 ft4">a) i Sverige:</P>
<P class="p41 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">den statliga inkomstskatten,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p42 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">kupongskatten,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p43 ft6"><SPAN class="ft6">3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">den s√§rskilda inkomstskatten f√∂r utomlands bosatta,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p44 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">4)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">den s√§rskilda inkomstskatten f√∂r utomlands bosatta artister m.fl., och</SPAN></P>
<P class="p45 ft4">5) den kommunala inkomstskatten,</P>
<P class="p46 ft4">(i det f√∂ljande ben√§mnda</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p35 ft4">Article 1</P>
<P class="p36 ft4">Personal scope</P>
<P class="p47 ft6">This Convention shall apply to persons who are residents of one or both of the Contracting States.</P>

<P class="p39 ft4">Taxes covered</P>

<P class="p68 ft4">Article 3</P>

<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p35 ft4">Article 4</P>
<P class="p36 ft4">Resident</P>
<P class="p47 ft9">(1) For the purposes of this Convention, the term ‚Äúresident of a Contracting State‚Äù means any person who, under the laws of that State, is liable to tax therein by reason of his domicile, residence, place of management or any other criterion of a similar nature, and also includes that State, a political subdivision, a local authority and any governmental body or agency thereof. However, in the case of a partnership or estate the term applies only to the extent that the income derived by such partnership or estate is subject to tax in that State as the income of a resident, either in its hands or in the hands of its partners or beneficiaries.</P>
<P class="p91 ft9">The term ‚Äúresident of a Contracting State‚Äù does not include any person who is liable to tax in that State in respect only of income from sources in that State.</P>
<P class="p92 ft9">(2) Where by reason of the provisions of paragraph (1) an individual is a resident of both Contracting States, then his status shall be determined as follows:</P>
<P class="p92 ft13">(a) he shall be deemed to be a resident only of the State in which he has a permanent home available to him; if he has a permanent home available to him in both States, he shall be deemed to be a</P>
<P class="p35 ft24">resident only of the State with</P>
<P class="p93 ft4">8</P>

<P class="p95 ft13"><SPAN class="ft6">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">om han stadigvarande vistas i b√•da staterna eller om han inte vistas stadigvarande i n√•gon av dem, anses han ha hemvist endast i den stat d√§r han √§r medborgare,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p96 ft13"><SPAN class="ft6">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">om han √§r medborgare i b√•da staterna eller om han inte √§r medborgare i n√•gon av dem, avg√∂r de beh√∂riga myndigheterna i de avtalsslutande staterna fr√•gan genom √∂msesidig √∂verenskommelse.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p99 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">if he has an habitual abode in both States or in neither of them, he shall be deemed to be a resident only of the State of which he is a national;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p92 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">if he is a national of both States or of neither of them, the competent authorities of the Contracting States shall settle the question by mutual agreement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p100 ft4">(3) Where by reason of the provisions of paragraph (1) a person other than an individual is a resident of both Contracting States, the competent authorities of the Contracting States shall endeavour to settle the question by mutual agreement. In such an agreement the competent authorities shall pay particular regard to where the place of effective management of the person is situated.</P>

<P class="p35 ft4">Article 6</P>
<P class="p39 ft4">Income from immovable property</P>
<P class="p119 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">Income derived by a resident of a Contracting State from immovable property (including income from agriculture or forestry) situated in the other Contracting State may be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p83 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">The term ‚Äúimmovable property‚Äù shall have the meaning which it has under the law of the Contracting State in which the property in question is situated. <P class="p120 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">The provisions of paragraph</SPAN></P>
<P class="p121 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft27">shall apply to income derived from the direct use, letting, or use in any other form of immovable property.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p122 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(4)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">The provisions of paragraphs</SPAN></P>
<P class="p123 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">and (3) shall also apply to the income from immovable property of an enterprise and to income from immovable property used for the performance of independent personal services.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p38 ft4">Article 8</P>
<P class="p39 ft4">Shipping and air transport</P>
<P class="p134 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">Profits of an enterprise of a Contracting State from the operation of ships or aircraft in international traffic shall be taxable only in that State.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p61 ft4">Artikel 10</P>
<P class="p36 ft4">Utdelning</P>
<P class="p37 ft4"><SPAN class="ft5">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">Utdelning fr√•n bolag med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat till person med hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten f√•r beskattas i denna andra stat.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p106 ft13"><SPAN class="ft5">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft12">Utdelningen f√•r emellertid beskattas √§ven i den avtalsslutande stat d√§r det bolag som betalar utdelningen har hemvist, enligt lag-</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p123 ft13">made or imposed between the two enterprises in their commercial or financial relations which differ from those which would be made between independent enterprises, then any profits which would, but for those conditions, have accrued to one of the enterprises, but, by reason of those conditions, have not so accrued, may be included in the profits of that enterprise and taxed accordingly.</P>
<P class="p71 ft13">(2) Where a Contracting State includes in the profits of an enterprise of that State ‚Äì and taxes accordingly ‚Äì profits on which an enterprise of the other Contracting State has been charged to tax in that other State and the profits so included are profits which would have accrued to the enterprise of the <NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State if the conditions made between the two enterprises had been those which would have been made between independent enterprises, then that other State shall make an appropriate adjustment to the amount of the tax charged therein on those profits, if it considers this adjustment to be justified. In determining such adjustment, due regard shall be had to the other provisions of this Convention and the competent authorities of the Contracting States shall if necessary consult each other.</P>
<P class="p140 ft4">Article 10</P>
<P class="p36 ft4">Dividends</P>
<P class="p119 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">Dividends paid by a company which is a resident of a Contracting State to a resident of the other Contracting State may be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p146 ft4">Article 11</P>

<P class="p134 ft4">(1) Interest arising in a Contracting State and beneficially owned by a resident of the other Contracting State shall be taxable only in that other State.</P>
<P class="p147 ft9">(2) The term ‚Äúinterest‚Äù as used in this Article means income from <NOBR>debt-claims</NOBR> of every kind, whether or not secured by mortgage and whether or not carrying a right to participate in the debtor‚Äôs profits, and in particular, income from government securities and income from bonds or debentures, including premiums and prizes attaching to such securities, bonds or debentures. <P class="p146 ft4">Article 13</P>
<P class="p36 ft4">Capital gains</P>
<P class="p47 ft9">(1) Gains derived by a resident of a Contracting State from the alienation of immovable property referred to in Article 6 and situated in the other Contracting State, or from the alienation of shares in a company the assets of which consist principally of such property, may be taxed in that other State.</P>
<P class="p158 ft9">(2) Gains from alienation of movable property forming part of the business property of a permanent establishment which an enterprise of a Contracting State has in the other Contracting State or of movable property pertaining to a fixed base available to a</P>

<P class="p35 ft4">Article 14</P>
<P class="p39 ft4">Independent personal services</P>
<P class="p119 ft13"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft12">Income derived by an individual who is a resident of a Contracting State in respect of professional services or other activities of an independent character shall be taxable only in that State unless he has a fixed base regularly available to him in the other Contracting State for the purpose of performing his activities. <P class="p162 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">The term ‚Äúprofessional services‚Äù includes especially independent scientific, literary, artistic, educational or teaching activities as well as the independent activities of physicians, lawyers, engineers, architects, dentists and accountants.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p68 ft4">Article 15</P>
<P class="p39 ft4">Dependent personal services</P>
<P class="p119 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">Subject to the provisions of Articles 16, 18 and 19, salaries, wages and other similar remuneration derived by a resident of a Contracting State in respect of an employment shall be taxable only in that State unless the employment is exercised in the other Contracting State. <P class="p36 ft4">Artistes and sportsmen</P>

<P class="p158 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">Where income in respect of personal activities exercised by an artiste or a sportsman in his capacity as such accrues not to the artiste or sportsman himself but to another person, that income may, notwithstanding the provisions of Articles 7, 14 and 15, be taxed in the Contracting State in which the activities of the artiste or sportsman are exercised.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p158 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraphs (1) and (2) income derived by an artiste or sportsman visiting a Contracting State from his personal activities as such shall be exempt from tax in that Contracting State where the activities are being exercised, if the activities are exercised within the framework of a visit which is substantially supported by the other Contracting State, a political subdivision, a local authority or a public institution thereof.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p35 ft4">Article 19</P>
<P class="p36 ft4">Government service</P>
<P class="p47 ft9">(1)(a) Remuneration, other than a pension, paid by a Contracting State or a political subdivision or a local authority thereof to an individual in respect of services rendered to that State or subdivision or authority shall be taxable only in that State.</P>
<P class="p100 ft9">(b) However, such remuneration shall be taxable only in the other Contracting State if the services are rendered in that State and the individual is a resident of that State who:</P>
<P class="p84 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">is a national of that State; or</SPAN></P>
<P class="p100 ft6"><SPAN class="ft6">(ii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft26">did not become a resident of that State solely for the purpose of rendering the services.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p170 ft9">(2) The provisions of Articles 15 and 16 shall apply to remuneration in respect of services rendered in connection with a business carried on by a Contracting State or a political subdivision or a local authority thereof.</P>

<P class="p35 ft4">Article 20</P>
<P class="p39 ft4">Students</P>
<P class="p119 ft13">Payments which a student or business apprentice who is or was immediately before visiting a Contracting State a resident of the other Contracting State and who is present in the <NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State solely for the purpose of his education or training receives for the purpose of his maintenance, education or training shall not be taxed in that State, provided that such payments arise from sources outside that State.</P>
<P class="p146 ft4">Article 21</P>
<P class="p39 ft4">Other income</P>
<P class="p119 ft13"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft12">Items of income of a resident of a Contracting State, wherever arising, not dealt with in the foregoing Articles of this Convention shall be taxable only in that State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p42 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">The provisions of paragraph</SPAN></P>
<P class="p123 ft13"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft40">shall not apply to income, other than income from immovable property as defined in paragraph (2) of Article 6, if the recipient of such income, being a resident of a Contracting State, carries on business in the other Contracting State through a permanent establishment situated therein, or performs in that other State independent personal services from a fixed base situated therein, and the right or property in respect of which the income is paid is effectively connected with such permanent establishment or fixed base. In such case the provisions of Article 7 or Article 14, as the case may be, shall apply.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p167 ft4">Undanr√∂jande av dubbelbeskattning</P>
<P class="p37 ft4">1. I fr√•ga om en person med hemvist i Sverige skall dubbelbeskattning undvikas p√• f√∂ljande s√§tt:</P>

<P class="p171 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">Om person med hemvist i Sverige f√∂rv√§rvar inkomst, som enligt best√§mmelserna i detta avtal beskattas endast i Polen, f√•r Sverige ‚Äì vid best√§mmandet av svensk progressiv skatt ‚Äì beakta s√•dan inkomst som beskattas endast i Polen.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p107 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft19">Utan hinder av best√§mmelserna i a) i denna punkt √§r utdelning fr√•n bolag med hemvist i Polen till bolag med hemvist i Sverige undantagen fr√•n svensk skatt enligt best√§mmelserna i svensk lag om skattebefrielse f√∂r utdelning som erh√•lls av svenska bolag fr√•n bolag utomlands.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p172 ft4">2. I fr√•ga om en person med hemvist i Polen skall dubbelbeskattning undvikas p√• f√∂ljande s√§tt:</P>

<P class="p36 ft4">Elimination of double taxation</P>
<P class="p173 ft4">(1) In the case of a resident of Sweden, double taxation shall be avoided as follows:</P>
<P class="p100 ft9"><SPAN class="ft5">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">Where a resident of Sweden derives income which under the laws of Poland and in accordance with the provisions of this Convention may be taxed in Poland, Sweden shall allow ‚Äì subject to the provisions of the laws of Sweden concerning credit for foreign tax (as it may be amended from time to time without changing the general principle hereof) ‚Äì as a deduction from the tax on such income, an amount equal to the Polish tax paid in respect of such income.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p174 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">Where a resident of Sweden derives income which, in accordance with the provisions of this Convention, shall be taxable only in Poland, Sweden may, when determining the graduated rate of Swedish tax, take into account the income which shall be taxable only in Poland.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p92 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">Notwithstanding the provisions of </SPAN><NOBR>sub-paragraph</NOBR> (a) of this paragraph, dividends paid by a company which is a resident of Poland to a company which is a resident of Sweden shall be exempt from Swedish tax according to the provisions of Swedish law governing the exemption of tax on dividends paid to Swedish companies by companies abroad.</P>
<P class="p175 ft4">(2) In the case of a resident of Poland, double taxation shall be avoided as follows:</P>
<P class="p137 ft30">(a) Where a resident of Poland</P>

<P class="p158 ft9">(b) Where a resident of Poland derives items of income which in accordance with the provisions of Articles 10 and 12, may be taxed in Sweden, Poland shall allow as a deduction from the tax on the income of that resident an amount equal to the income tax paid in Sweden. <P class="p68 ft4">Article 23</P>
<P class="p36 ft4"><NOBR>Non-discrimination</NOBR></P>
<P class="p47 ft9">(1) Nationals of a Contracting State shall not be subjected in the other Contracting State to any taxation or any requirement connected therewith, which is other or more burdensome than the taxation and connected requirements to which nationals of that other State in the same circumstances are or may be subjected. This provision shall, notwithstanding the provisions of Article 1, also apply to persons who are not residents of one or both of the Contracting States.</P>

<P class="p38 ft4">Article 24</P>
<P class="p36 ft4">Mutual agreement procedure</P>
<P class="p185 ft45"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft44">Where a person considers that the actions of one or both of the Contracting States result or will result for him in taxation not in accordance with the provisions of this Convention, he may, irrespective of the remedies provided by the domestic law of those States, present his case to the competent authority of the Contracting State of which he is a resident or, if his case comes under paragraph</SPAN></P>
<P class="p121 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft46">of Article 23, to that of the Contracting State of which he is a national. The case must be presented within three years from the first notification of the action resulting in taxation not in accordance with the provisions of the Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p162 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">The competent authority shall endeavour, if the objection appears to it to be justified and if it is not itself able to arrive at a satisfactory solution, to resolve the case by mutual agreement with the competent authority of the other Contracting State, with a view to the avoidance of taxation which is not in accordance with the Convention. Any agreement reached shall be implemented notwithstanding any time limits in the domestic law of the Contracting States.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p68 ft4">Article 25</P>
<P class="p39 ft4">Exchange of information</P>
<P class="p119 ft13"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft12">The competent authorities of the Contracting States shall exchange such information as is foreseeably relevant for carrying out the provisions of this Convention or of the administration or enforcement of the domestic laws concerning taxes of every kind and description imposed on behalf of the Contracting States, or of their political subdivisions or local authorities, insofar as the taxation thereunder is not contrary to the Convention. <P class="p71 ft13"><SPAN class="ft6">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft12">Any information received under paragraph (1) by a Contracting State shall be treated as secret in the same manner as information obtained under the domestic laws of that State and shall be disclosed only to persons or authorities (including courts and administrative bodies) concerned with the assessment or collection of, the enforcement or prosecution in respect of, the determination of appeals in relation to the taxes referred to in paragraph (1), or the</SPAN></P>

<P class="p38 ft4">Article 26</P>
<P class="p191 ft4">Assistance in the collection of taxes</P>
<P class="p119 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">The Contracting States shall lend assistance to each other in the collection of revenue claims. This assistance is not restricted by Articles 1 and 2. The competent authorities of the Contracting States may by mutual agreement settle the mode of application of this Article.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p83 ft13"><SPAN class="ft6">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft12">The term ‚Äúrevenue claim‚Äù as used in this Article means an amount owed in respect of taxes of every kind and description imposed on behalf of the Contracting States, or of their political subdivisions or local authorities, insofar as the taxation thereunder is not contrary to this Convention or any other instrument to which the Contracting States are parties, as well as interest, administrative penalties and costs of collection or conservancy related to such amount.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p71 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">When a revenue claim of a Contracting State is enforceable under the laws of that State and is owed by a person who, at that time, cannot, under the laws of that State, prevent its collection, that revenue claim shall, at the request of the competent authority of that State, be accepted for purposes of collection by the competent authority of the other Contracting State. <P class="p96 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(4)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">When a revenue claim of a Contracting State is a claim in respect of which that State may, under its law, take measures of conservancy with a view to ensure its collection, that revenue claim shall, at the request of the competent authority of that State, be accepted for purposes of taking measures of conservancy by the competent authority of the other Contracting State. <P class="p114 ft9"><SPAN class="ft6">(5)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft34">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraphs (3) and (4) a revenue claim accepted by a Contracting State for purposes of paragraph (3) or (4) shall not, in that State, be subject to the time limits or accorded any priority applicable to a revenue claim under the laws of that State by reason of its nature as such. <P class="p96 ft9">(a) in the case of a request under paragraph (3), a revenue claim of the <NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State that is enforceable under the laws of that State and is owed by a person who, at that time, cannot, under the laws of that State, prevent its collection, or</P>
<P class="p198 ft4">(b) in the case of a request under paragraph (4), a revenue claim of the <NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State in respect of which that State may, under its laws, take measures of conservancy with a view to ensure its collection</P>
<P class="p95 ft13">the competent authority of the <NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State shall promptly notify the competent authority of the other State of that fact and, at the option of the other State, the <NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State shall either suspend or withdraw its request.</P>
<P class="p199 ft4"><SPAN class="ft6">(8)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">In no case shall the provisions of this Article be construed so as to impose on a Contracting State the obligation:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p95 ft13">(a) to carry out administrative measures at variance with the laws and administrative practice of that or of the other Contracting State;</P>
<P class="p200 ft4">(b) to carry out measures which would be contrary to public policy (ordre public);</P>
<P class="p96 ft13">(c) to provide assistance if the other Contracting State has not pursued all reasonable measures of collection or conservancy, as the case may be, available under its</P>

<P class="p47 ft4">Notwithstanding any other provisions of this Convention, where</P>

<P class="p35 ft4">Article 30</P>
<P class="p39 ft4">Termination</P>
<P class="p119 ft9">This Convention shall remain in force until terminated by a Contracting State.
